  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=7.4)
    The story demonstrates significant originality in its integration of academic theory with magical elements. The language generally avoids clichés and purple prose, maintaining a consistent tone throughout. There's some overreliance on adjective pairs ("frantic peace," "infinite moment") that border on being too ornate, and certain phrases like "the city held its breath" verge on familiar territory. However, the narrative succeeds in creating a fresh concept with its temporal mirror theory.
